 Chinese smartphone company Realme has announced Realme YO Days Sale
 is dauraan company ke smartfones par dils or discount die jaaenge
 This cell company is organized in the joy of completing 60 lakh user base
 cell kii shuruyaat aaj yani 9 april se ho rahi he or ye cell 12 april tak jari rahegi
 During the sale, customers will get offers on Realme 3, Realme 2 Pro, Realme U1 and Realme C1 smartphones
 saath hi is dauraan flash cell kaa bhi aayojan kiya ja rahaa he
 Apart from the company's website, customers can also take advantage of Realme Yo Days Sale from Flipkart and Amazon
 company cell ke dauraan do baar apane Realme Bagpack ko 1 rupee main cell karegi
 This sale will be on April 9 at 11:50 AM and also on April 11 at 11:50 AM
 cell ke dauraan Realme 3 kii baat karen to ise aaj yani 9 april ko ek baar phir se cell main uplabdh karaayaa jayega
 Its sale will be on Flipkart and Reality's website
 saath hi isaki flash cell 11 april ko bhi hogi
 Talking about Realme 2 Pro, it will be made available with a discount of Rs 1,000 during the sale
 ye discount smartphone ke saare verients par diya jayega
 Customers will also get a prepaid offer of Rs 1,000 on Flipkart with this smartphone
 preeped ofer ke tahat 4GB+64GB verient 10,990 rupee main, 6GB+64GB verient 12,990 rupee main or 8GB+128GB verient main 14,990 rupee milegaa
 The first 500 customers to buy this smartphone on Rilaymi's website will get free reality buds
 graahak is ofer kaa phiga 10 april ko 11 am se le paaenge
 Talking about Realme U1, customers will be able to buy this smartphone from 12 noon on April 10 at an initial price of Rs 9,999 from Amazon's website
 ye keemat base verient 3GB+64GB kii hogi
 At the same time, customers will be able to buy 4GB + 64GB variants for Rs 10,999
 cell ke dauraan donon verients par amejan par 1,000 rupee kaa preeped ofer bhi milegaa
 In this case, both variants can be purchased for Rs 8,999 and Rs 9,999 respectively
 10 april ko rialami kii website se Realme U1 ke nae 3GB + 64GB verient ko kharidne vaale pehle 500 graahakon ko free rialami yearbads milegaa
